 If you keep the roof of the house good, then the 12th house is also considered to be good
 ghar kii chat kai prakaar kii hoti he
 When we are talking about the ceiling, it means that one is the ceiling inside your room where there are fans etc
 and the other is the roof which is called Gucci or upper ceiling
 aao jaanate hai ki ghar kii upree chat kisi hona chahie
 The roofs are mainly of three types - flat roof, sloping roof and round roof
 teenon hi chat vaastu anusaar bane to behatar he
 More floors can be built above the flat roof, but this is not possible in sloping roofs
 haalanki kuch makaan aise hote hai jisamen samaat or dhaalu donon hi prakaar kii chhaton kaa upyog kiya jaataa he
 Sloping roofs are often formed in areas with high rainfall or snowfall
 shaharon main adhiktar sapaat chhaton vaale makaan hote hai
 The thing to keep in mind in these terraces is which side the slope should be
 chat yaa ghar ke farsh kaa dhalaan vaastu anusaar rakhana chahie
 There should be a slope from southwest to north-east
 ghar kii chat kaa dhalaan iske vipareet nahin hona chahie
 Now the question arises what to do if someone has a west or south facing house
 iske liye kisi vaastushastri se milakar sthaan ko dekhakar hi dhalaan kidar hona chahie, yah tay hoga
 There should not be any kind of shaving in the roof of the house
 jaise aajkal ghar kii chat main log do-bai-do kaa ek hissaa khaali chhod dete hai ujaale ke liye
 This will always maintain air pressure in the house, which will have a bad effect on health and mind and brain
 tirchhi chat banane se bachein- chat ke nirmaan main is baat kaa dhyaan rakhen ki vah tirchhi dizin vaali na hon
 This causes other health problems
 ghar kii chat kii oonchai bhi vaastu anusaar hona chahie
 If height 8
 5 foot se kam hoti he to yah aapke liye kai tarah kii samasyaayein lekar aati he or jivan main aage badhanaa aapke liye mushkil ho jayega he
 If the house is small, the ceiling height should be at least 10 to 12 feet
 ghar kii chat par kisi bhi prakaar kii gandagi na karen
 Do not keep any kind of bamboo or waste items here
 jin logon ke gharon kii chat par anupayogi saamaan rakhaa hota he, vahaan nakaaratmak shaktiyaan adhik sakriy rahati hai
 People living in that house have negative views
 parivaar main bhi manmutav kii sthitiyaan nirmit hoti hai
 It is important to know in which direction the water tank is placed on the roof of the house
 uttar-purv disha pani kaa tanks rakhane ke liye uchit nahin he, isse tanaav badhata he or padhane-likhane main bacchon kaa man nahin lagata he
 The south-east direction is the direction of fire, therefore it is also not considered suitable for placing a water tank
 agni or pani kaa mail hone se gambhir vaastudosh utpann hota he
 According to Vastu science, it is auspicious to be higher and heavier than south-west ie south west corner
 kai makaanon main purv yaa uttar disha ke makaanon mentand bana liye jate hai or attala bhar diya jaataa he, jabaki is prakaar karne se anek kashton kaa saamana bhi karnaa padataa he or hamen iskaa bhaan tak nahin hota he
 It is often seen that whatever is in our house, it is kept in northeast or northeast
 kabhi-kabhi mashin bhi is disha main rakh di jaati he
 In such a situation, we get loss rather than profit and we have to face continuous loss
 ham yadi dakshin-pashchim main taand banaaen to saamaan rakhane main adhik suvidha hokar anaavashyak pareshaaniyon se bachaa ja saktaa he
 Similarly, if the machine or heavy object is kept in south direction from igneous angle to south west angle, then it will run more smoothly

 Research has shown that children with vitamin d levels higher than 80 nmol / l (nanomol) per liter have lower low-density lipoprotein (LDL) or children with vitamin levels less than 50 nmol / liter
 Bad cholesterol level occurs
 50enemoel / litre ko vitamin di paryaaptta kii seemaa mana jaataa he
 This research has been published in the Journal of Clinical Endocrinology and Metabolism
 isamen eastern finland vishvavidhyalay ke shodhakartaaon ne kareeb 500 bacchon ke aankadon kaa vishleshan kiya he

 78 karod11 Prime Minister Narendra Modi attended the National Youth Parliament Festival 2019 on Wednesday
 vigyaan bhawan main yojit is kaarykram ko sambodhit karte hue piem modi ne kaha ki saathiyon main aap jaise urjavan logon se jab bhi miltaa hum, mere bheetar bhi josh bhar jaataa he
 You have been discussing important issues related to the country and society for the last two days
 charchaa or samvaad kii yah prakriya, desh ke janatantr ko shashakt karti he
 Addressing the Youth Parliament Honor Ceremony, PM Modi said that we need to bring new ideas, ideas that connect the society and the country
 unhone kaha ki mere saamne new india kii tasviir he
 People who are bound in syllabus do not come here
 yahaan agar aap log aae hai to iskaa matlab he ki aap silebus ke baahar bhi dekhte or padhate hai
 Because the goods served are messed up
 isliye mujhe yakeen he ki aap parose hue maal ke alaava bhi dekhte hai
 Hopefully, you will not have received anything served young, but you will find it yourself
 binova bhaave kehete the ki a-sarkari chijen asarkaari hoti hai
 PM Modi said that in this century there is no communicator greater than Mahatma Gandhi
 piem modi ne kaha ki hamaare munh se niklaa hua shabd sahi jagah par tir kii tarah janaa chahie
 Our voice may be impressive or not, but it must be inspiring
 pradhanmantri narendra modi ne 'rashtriya yuva sansad samaaroh 2019' ke dauraan kaha ki main lambi planning se kaam karata hum
 i believe in working under continuous process
 tokanism main meraa vishwaas nahin he
 Addressing the 'national Youth Parliament Festival 2019' held at Vigyan Bhawan, Delhi, Prime Minister Narendra Modi said, "the country should know what their elected MP is doing
" "is kaarykram main kuch aise suzav aae hai, jinhen vistaar dekar desh main chal rahi yojanaon par sudhaar kiya ja saktaa he
 Average productivity in the 16th Lok Sabha was 85 percent
 kareeb 205 bill paas hue
 The 16th Lok Sabha did 20 percent more work than the 15th Lok Sabha
 lekin main isse santusht nahin hum
 If Modi is there then it should be 200 percent
 piem modi ne kaha ki agar hamaare desh or samaaj main aisi yuva peedi taiyaar hoti he jo samaaj ke muddon par sahi tareeke se sochakar samaaj ko apni baat bataate hai to samaaj kaa man banane main bahut badi bhoomika adaa kar sakate hai
 PM Modi said that a poet had said: He is missing that my flight is less, i am sure that this sky is less
 yuva nae ideas se, freshness se bharaa hua hota he
 He is not burdened by the past, so he is more able to deal with challenges and problems
 dilli ke chidyaghar (neshnal zoological park) main marane vaale hiranon kii taadaad 36 tak bataai ja rahi he
 The Xu administration confirmed 17 deer died of rabies
 lagaataar hiranon kii maut se ju prashasan ne rashtriya rog niyantran centre (NCDC) se turant madad kii guhaar lagaai he
 Appeal for help from NCDC a letter has been written to the NCDC on May 18 by the Zoo Authority, referring to the growing outbreak of rabies at the zoo
 ju athurity kii maane to rebies kaa khatra ab chidyaghar main kaam karne vaale logon par madraane laga he
 The situation is getting worse day by day rather than under control
 ju prashasan ke mutabik paaltu jaanwaron main faile rogon ko kaabo main karne ke liye tamaam upaay kiye jo vahaan uplabdh hai, lekin halaat nahin sudhar rahe hai
 After which, now the administration has written a letter to the NCDC for help
 14 farvari se maut kaa silsilaa jariju athurity ke mutabik 14 farvari 2016 ko dilli jal board ke siver kaa pani hiran ke baade main ghus gaya tha
 After which the dirty water was removed, but after that suddenly three thrillers died
 postmortem report main pataa chalaa ki is hiranon ne us siver ke gande pani ko piyaa tha
 The Zoo administration sent samples of dead deer to the Indian Veterinary Research Institute (IVRI) to find out the cause of death
 jaanch main pataa chalaa ki hiranon kii maut rebies kii vajah se hui
 Since then, other animals in the zoo are constantly being investigated so that they do not fall prey to this rabies
 ju prashasan par bhi laaparvaahee kaa aaropahaalanki hiranon kii maut ko lekarju prashasanpar bhi sawaal uth rahe hai
 The Xu administration is accused of not taking the matter seriously in the beginning
 saath hi laaparvaahee kii vajah se hiranon kii maut kaa aankada badhane kaa aarope he
 Now that the situation has become very serious, the Zoo administration has become active
 sabase bada khatra ye he ki is rebies kii chapet main kahin insaan na aa jaae
 Because about 8 to 10 thousand people come to visit the zoo every day
